) AS [t]

    FROM [Canteens] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[Id] = @__canteenId_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[CanteenId], [m].[CategoryId], [m].[DailyMenuId], [m].[Description], [m].[Disponibility], [m].[Name], [m].[PictureURL], [m].[PortionId], [m].[Price], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CategoryName], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[PortionName]

) AS [t]
